Directly inspired by The Climate Fresk, The Agri'Food Collage is a scientific and creative workshop designed to acquire as a team an overview of the issues weighing on our food supply, and discuss the actions to be taken to turn it into a solutions platform.\nDeveloped in partnership with ADEME \u2013 the French agency for the ecological transition, The Agri'Food Collage is based on over 150 reference documents and the contribution of experts from the many fields related to our food: environment, economy, society, ... and a bit of history too! See it as the agri-food system \"serious game\", based on collective intelligence and extremely educational because it allows you to learn a lot in a very short time, whether you're just curious or already knowledgeable.\nIt is also an opportunity to meet other people interested in the subject of the sustainability of our food, and to discover an effective tool to raise awareness and catalyze transformative action around you.\nAgenda & Practical Info\n  Workshop language : English.\n  Group introduction\nReconstruction of the Agri'Food Collage\nDebrief\nShare actions ideas\n  Recommended age: 16 and above.\nThis workshop will be held online via videoconference, and we'll be using a web-based visual collaboration tool. Please make sure you have: \na good Internet connection\nuse a computer (no tablets or cell phones) equipped with a microphone (mandatory) and a camera (recommended), and preferably have a wheel mouse at hand. \nAll technical details will be sent to registered participants by e-mail.\nThis session is primarily intended for individuals.\nIf you want to organize a workshop for your teams, we offer dedicated sessions adapted to your needs: contact us!\nTo know more about The Agri'Food Collage\n  Project website\nFollow us on Facebook or LinkedIn\n  You can't make it on that date? How can companies evolve their business models?\nTo discover the answers to these and many other questions, come and take part in a workshop of the Circular Economy Collage. The workshop covers topics such as climate change, biodiversity loss, resource scarcity and pollution generated by human activities and enables you to identify concrete courses of action!\nAbout the workshop\nThe Circular Economy Collage is a stimulating, group-based workshop founded on scientific information, which enables participants to grasp the limits of our existing global \u201clinear\u201d economy and understand the opportunities offered by the circular economy. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",
